National Association of Realtors-India ( NAR-India )
The Credible Voice of Incredible Realtors
The Journey of a Thousand Miles begins with a single step. And the only tribe that covers every square foot of the thousand miles is a Realtor, a Real Estate Agent, or a Real Estate Broker. May the tribe grow.
Mr. Sumanth Reddy (President) and Mr. Samir Arora (Hon. Secretary) will address the Nation                     ( of Realtors, Brokers, Agents ) at 5 pm ( not 8 pm :) , on Tuesday, 2nd June, 2020 and will take Questions from the Fraternity on any subject related to Real Estate and answer them all.
A Webinar that will add value to every Real Estate Professional, whether you are a one man army or an army of many, whether you are from a Big City or from a very small Town in India, whether you manage Residential, Commercial, Industrial or Lands segment in Real Estate, whether you are an established pro or a fresh starter or aspiring Real Estate professional.
If you possess these two qualifications,
1.	You are a Real Estate Professional in India ( LOCAL ) &
2.	You want your Voice to be heard ( VOCAL )
You cannot afford to miss this Webinar. Register now at the link given below. The Zoom Webinar will have special features on Zoom for participants that will not be available on Facebook Live transmission of the same webinar.
Questions Raised till now
1.	What does the future hold for Real Estate Industry ? 
2.	What does the future look like for a Realtor ? 
3.	How should a Realtor change and adapt to the changing circumstances in the Industry ?
4.	Why is it a must for every Real Estate professional in India to be a member of NAR-India ? 
5.	How does one join a local city or state association to become a part of NAR-India ? What if your city or state does not have a Real Estate association that is member of NAR-India ? 
6.	How does NAR-India deliver value to a Real estate professional in a metro/big city vis a vis a smaller town or remote place ? 
7.	How does NAR-India represent Brokerâ€™s Interest with the Central and State Government and RERA authorities ? 
8.	How will NAR-India help counter the Disruptors in Real Estate markets in India ? 
9.	How will NAR-India help against the mandated business of IPCs ? 
10.	How can every Real Estate professional add value to him/herself, the Industry and the Country by becoming a member of NAR-India ?
To know the answers to these and any more questions or suggestions you may have, Join the one of a kind Webinar from NAR-India, BE VOCAL for LOCAL, in a freewheeling conversation between the Game Changers, the President and the Hon. Secretary of NAR-India.

*YOUR CREA(I) WHATSAPP GROUP POSTINGS* 

Inspite of our repeated requests for our members to strictly adhere to our WhatsApp group Guidelines, some are either not aware of it or just do not follow.

For the benefit of our members in particular and as an Association in general, we highlight once again the following guidelines to be strictly followed while posting messages in *Your CREA (I) WhatsApp group.*

1) *TIMINGS FOR POSTINGS*
        
        Strictly 8.00 AM to 9.00 PM

2) *WHAT TO POST*

      Only messages related to Real Estate and should be consolidated as one at a time.

3) *PHOTOS*

Maximum of 2 photos related to Real Estate inventories and no photos/videos of builders/Developers projects as a backdrop or in the interest of promoting their projects as a whole.

Members are requested to strictly follow the above guidelines and *VIOLATION* of it will invite delisting from the Group for a Week and repeat of it for 2 weeks.

Please Cooperate.
